[{"bookPath":"","title":"Error Codes","titleId":"ref-error-codes","hasOtp":true,"hasPageHeader":true},"<p>\n  <i id=\"p_0\" class=\"pid\"></i>This section provides an in depth explanation of the error codes produced from\n  the Reach compiler.<a href=\"#p_0\" class=\"pid\">0</a>\n</p>\n<h2 id=\"RA0000\" class=\"refHeader\">RA0000<a aria-hidden=\"true\" tabindex=\"-1\" href=\"#RA0000\"><span class=\"icon icon-link\"></span></a></h2>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_1\" class=\"pid\"></i>This error indicates that a program, targeting the Algorand connector, is attempting to\n  transfer a <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_Token\" title=\"rsh: Token\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">Token</span></a></span> in the same consensus step it was created in. It is impossible\n  to perform this action because one must opt-in to receive a token on Algorand. To opt-in, one must\n  know the id, however the id of the token cannot be known until after the transaction that created it.<a href=\"#p_1\" class=\"pid\">1</a>\n</p>\n<p><i id=\"p_2\" var(--shiki-color-text)\">informOfTokenId</span></span> by utilizing\n  <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/frontend/#js_acc\" title=\"js: acc\"><span style=\"color: href=\"#RA0001\"><span class=\"icon icon-link\"></span></a></h2>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_5\" class=\"pid\"></i>This error indicates that a program, targeting the Algorand connector, is attempting to pay a <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_Token\" title=\"rsh: Token\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">Token</span></a></span> at the same time it is published.\n  It is impossible to perform this action because one must opt-in to receive a token on Algorand.\n  To opt-in, one must know the id, however the application cannot learn the application until after it has received the publication, which must occur after all pay transactions.<a href=\"#p_5\" class=\"pid\">5</a>\n</p>\n<p><i id=\"p_6\" class=\"pid\"></i>The following code has this error:<a href=\"#p_6\" class=\"pid\">6</a></p>\n<pre class=\"snippet numbered\"><div class=\"codeHeader\">&nbsp;<a class=\"far fa-copy copyBtn\" data-clipboard-text=\"Alice.publish(tok).pay([[5, tok]]);\ncommit();\" class=\"pid\">7</a>\n</p>\n<pre class=\"snippet numbered\"><div class=\"codeHeader\">&nbsp;<a class=\"far fa-copy copyBtn\" data-clipboard-text=\"Alice.publish(tok);\ncommit();\nAlice.pay([[5, var(--shiki-token-function)\">f</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">();</span></li></ol></pre>\n<h2 id=\"RE0001\" class=\"refHeader\">RE0001<a aria-hidden=\"true\" tabindex=\"-1\" href=\"#RE0001\"><span class=\"icon icon-link\"></span></a></h2>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_15\" class=\"pid\"></i>This error indicates that a program uses an invalid assignment operator.\n  Reach only supports assignment using the <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">=</span></span> operator. Any other operator,\n  such as <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">+=</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">*=</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">...</span></span> is not allowed.<a href=\"#p_15\" class=\"pid\">15</a>\n</p>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_16\" class=\"pid\"></i>For example, the code below erroneously tries to re-assign <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">x</span></span> at the end of\n  a <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/consensus/#rsh_while\" title=\"rsh: while\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">while</span></a></span> loop:<a href=\"#p_16\" class=\"pid\">16</a>\n</p>\n<pre class=\"snippet numbered\"><div class=\"codeHeader\">&nbsp;<a class=\"far fa-copy copyBtn\" data-clipboard-text=\"x *= 2;\ncontinue;\" href=\"#\"></a></div><ol class=\"snippet\"><li value=\"1\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">x </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">*=</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">2</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">;</span></li><li value=\"2\"><a href=\"/rsh/consensus/#rsh_continue\" title=\"rsh: href=\"/rsh/consensus/#rsh_var\" title=\"rsh: var\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">var</span></a></span> and immediately\n  before a <span class=\"snip\"><a differs in the continuation of a\n  branching statement. That is, if a Reach program may execute multiple different code paths at\n  runtime, the continuation of those branches must make the same assumption about state.<a href=\"#p_186\" class=\"pid\">186</a>\n</p>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_187\" class=\"pid\"></i>For example, this error may be caused by having one branch end in consensus step and\n  the other in a step. tabindex=\"-1\" href=\"#RE0080\"><span class=\"icon icon-link\"></span></a></h2>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_227\" class=\"pid\"></i>This error indicates that there is an attempt to conditionally transition to consensus\n  without a <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/step/#rsh_timeout\" title=\"rsh: timeout\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">timeout</span></a></span>. When making a conditional publication, such as <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">A</span><a href=\"/rsh/step/#rsh_publish\" title=\"rsh: publish\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">.publish</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">(x)</span><a href=\"/rsh/step/#rsh_when\" title=\"rsh: when\"><span style=\"color: class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">shouldPublish</span></span> is not statically <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_true\" title=\"rsh: true\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">true</span></a></span>.<a href=\"#p_227\" class=\"pid\">227</a>\n</p>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_228\" class=\"pid\"></i>In <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/consensus/#rsh_parallelReduce\" title=\"rsh: parallelReduce\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">parallelReduce</span></a></span> or <span class=\"snip\"><a Participant\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">Participant</span></a></span>\n  always races, the <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/step/#rsh_when\" title=\"rsh: when\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">when</span></a></span> field in their <code>PUBLISH_EXPR</code> is statically <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_true\" title=\"rsh: true\"><span able to <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/step/#rsh_publish\" title=\"rsh: publish\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">publish</span></a></span> both <code>wager</code> and <code>deadline</code>, and pay the <code>wager</code> because the contract has already been created.<a href=\"#p_297\" class=\"pid\">297</a>\n</p>\n<h2 id=\"RE0103\" class=\"refHeader\">RE0103<a aria-hidden=\"true\" tabindex=\"-1\" href=\"#RE0103\"><span class=\"icon icon-link\"></span></a></h2>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_298\" class=\"pid\"></i>This error indicates that you are attempting to <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/step/#rsh_publish\" title=\"rsh: publish\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">publish</span></a></span> a <span class=\"snip\"><a title=\"rsh: while\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">while</span></a></span> loop. This is not currently possible in Reach. You must publish <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_Token\" title=\"rsh: Token\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">Token</span></a></span>\n  values outside of loops.<a style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">View</span></a></span> cannot be exposed. Every\n  <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/appinit/#rsh_View\" title=\"rsh: View\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">View</span></a></span> must explicitly state the <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">Type</span></span> of function arguments it accepts.<a href=\"#p_312\" class=\"pid\">312</a>\n</p>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_313\" class=\"pid\"></i>If your <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/appinit/#rsh_View\" title=\"rsh: View\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">View</span></a></span> function relies on a varying number of arguments or <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">Type</span></span>s, you\n  can either abstract the arguments into a new <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_Data\" title=\"rsh: Data\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">Data</span></a></span> type or make separate <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/appinit/#rsh_View\" tabindex=\"-1\" href=\"#RE0128\"><span class=\"icon icon-link\"></span></a></h2>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_371\" class=\"pid\"></i>This error indicates that you are attempting to update loop variables to a <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_Tuple\" title=\"rsh: Tuple\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">Tuple</span></a></span> of different length.\n  This error can occur in the assignments before a <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/consensus/#rsh_while\" title=\"rsh: while\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">while</span></a></span> loop's <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/consensus/#rsh_continue\" title=\"rsh: continue\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">continue</span></a></span>, or the <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_return\" title=\"rsh: return\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">return</span></a></span> expression in a <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/consensus/#rsh_parallelReduce\" title=\"rsh: parallelReduce\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">parallelReduce</span></a></span> case.<a href=\"#p_371\" class=\"pid\">371</a>\n</p>\n<p><i id=\"p_372\" class=\"pid\"></i>The code below erroneously attempts to update the loop variable to a 2-tuple in the timeout, although the loop variable is a 1-tuple:<a href=\"#p_372\" class=\"pid\">372</a></p>\n<pre class=\"snippet numbered\"><div class=\"codeHeader\">&nbsp;<a class=\"far fa-copy copyBtn\" data-clipboard-text=\"const [ a ] =\n  parallelReduce([ true ])\n  .invariant(balance() == 0)\n  .while(a)\n  .case(A,\n    () => ({\n        when: declassify(interact.when()),\n    }),\n    (_) => {\n      return [ false ];\n    })\n    .timeout(relativeSecs(10), () => {\n      Anybody.publish();\n      return [ true, 43 ];\n    });\" href=\"#\"></a></div><ol class=\"snippet\"><li value=\"1\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_const\" style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">.</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">i</span><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_set\" title=\"rsh: set\"><span style=\"color: href=\"/rsh/consensus/#rsh_commit\" title=\"rsh: commit\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">commit</span></a></span> in its scope.\n  Since, there are no <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/consensus/#rsh_commit\" title=\"rsh: commit\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">commit</span></a></span>s between <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: title=\"rsh: set\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">.set</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">(i)</span></span> and <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/consensus/#rsh_continue\" title=\"rsh: continue\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">continue</span></a></span>, which is the end of the lexical scope, there is no\n  way to observe the effect of setting <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">I</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">.i</span></span>.<a href=\"#p_402\" class=\"pid\">402</a>\n</p>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_403\" class=\"pid\"></i>You can generally fix this error by inserting a <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/consensus/#rsh_commit\" title=\"rsh: title=\"rsh: View\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">View</span></a></span> to be observable. In the case of a <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/consensus/#rsh_while\" title=\"rsh: while\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">while</span></a></span> loop, like the\n  program above, it can be fixed the following way:<a href=\"#p_403\" class=\"pid\">403</a>\n</p>\n<pre class=\"snippet numbered\"><div class=\"codeHeader\">&nbsp;<a class=\"far fa-copy copyBtn\" an API caller relies on non-consensus state to operate.\n  Typically, this is because the <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/local/#rsh_assume\" title=\"rsh: assume\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">Struct</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">( [ [</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-string-expression)\">\"a1\"</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> UInt] ] ) }); </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-comment)\">// View produces a Struct</span></li></ol></pre>\n<h2 id=\"RW0006\" class=\"refHeader\">RW0006<a aria-hidden=\"true\" tabindex=\"-1\" href=\"#RW0006\"><span class=\"icon icon-link\"></span></a></h2>\n<p><i id=\"p_473\" class=\"pid\"></i>This warning indicates that you referenced network seconds in your program.<a href=\"#p_473\" class=\"pid\">473</a></p>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_474\" class=\"pid\"></i>On most consensus networks, network seconds are completely unrelated to reality.\n  The only invariant about these timestamps are that they never go down and they never increase by more than a fixed amont of seconds at each increment.\n  (For example, on Ethereum, the fixed amount is 15, and on Algorand the amount\n  is 25.\n  Typically these are configurable parameters of the consensus, but have never\n  actually been changed.)<a href=\"#p_474\" class=\"pid\">474</a>\n</p>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_475\" class=\"pid\"></i>For example, time 20 could actually occur on Monday at 17:45:00, but be assigned the timestamp of Sunday at 05:08:32, because that's when time 19 was and there was network downtime.\n  Furthermore, if time 21 was \"on time\" and actually occurred on Monday at 17:45:05, it would be assigned to Sunday at 05:08:57 (25 seconds after time 20's assignment).<a href=\"#p_475\" class=\"pid\">475</a>\n</p>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_476\" class=\"pid\"></i>This process would slowly \"resychronize\"; on Algorand, it would gain 20 seconds on the \"actual time\" every 5 second round.\n  This means it would take roughly 5 hours to resychronize after a day of downtime.\n  However, this is not guaranteed to occur at any particular time, because block proposers (on Algorand, at least) are free to leave the timestamp unchanged from the last block (i.e. there is no minimum increment), so it is possible that time would never be synchronized with reality at all.<a href=\"#p_476\" class=\"pid\">476</a>\n</p>\n<p><i id=\"p_477\" class=\"pid\"></i>Thus, it is unsafe to rely on network seconds for most purposes (such as interest on loans, time limits on auctions, and so forth), because network downtime (even intermitten) and adversarial block proposers (acting alone) can delay and influence the block time.<a href=\"#p_477\" class=\"pid\">477</a></p>\n<h3 id=\"problematic-code-2\" class=\"refHeader\">Problematic code:<a aria-hidden=\"true\" tabindex=\"-1\" href=\"#problematic-code-2\"><span class=\"icon icon-link\"></span></a></h3>\n<pre class=\"snippet numbered\"><div class=\"codeHeader\">&nbsp;<a class=\"far fa-copy copyBtn\" data-clipboard-text=\"relativeSecs(t) // references network seconds\nabsoluteSecs(t) // references network seconds\nlastConsensusSecs() // references network seconds\" href=\"#\"></a></div><ol class=\"snippet\"><li value=\"1\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_relativeSecs\" title=\"rsh: relativeSecs\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">relativeSecs</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">(t) style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">absoluteSecs</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">(t) </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-comment)\">// references network seconds</span></li><li value=\"3\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_lastConsensusSecs\" title=\"rsh: lastConsensusSecs\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">lastConsensusSecs</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">() </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-comment)\">// references network seconds</span></li></ol></pre>\n<h3 id=\"correct-code-2\"
